<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подсветить.html>подсвети́ть</a> (17550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:светить.html>свети́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svetítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсветить.html>подсвети́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podsvetítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсвечивать.html>подсве́чивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to illuminate, to highlight <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from below or from the side</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to light slightly or additionally</li></ol>

***подсветка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подсветка.html>подсве́тка</a> (22600)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсветить.html>подсвети́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podsvetítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсветка.html>подсве́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podsvétka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсветка.html>подсве́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсветка.html>подсве́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсветка.html>подсве́ток</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>light, lighting, illumination, booster light, accent light, micro-light
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подсветка.html>подсве́тка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сзади.html>сза́ди</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podsvétka</b> szádi</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">rear illumination</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подсветка.html>подсве́тка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спереди.html>спе́реди</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podsvétka</b> spéredi</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">front illumination</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подсветка.html>подсве́тка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>це́ли</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podsvétka</b> céli</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">target illumination</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informatics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> highlight</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подсвечивать.html>подсве́чивать</a> (31583)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсветить.html>подсвети́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podsvetítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсвечивать.html>подсве́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podsvéčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсветить.html>подсвети́ть</a></b>)

<li>to light slightly or additionally</li></ol>

***подсесть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подсесть.html>подсе́сть</a> (8981)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сесть.html>сесть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсесть.html>подсе́сть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podséstʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подса́живаться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take a seat <i>(next to)</i>, to sit down <i>(next to)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get hooked <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсесть.html>подсе́сть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:игла.html>иглу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podséstʹ na iglú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) to take to the needle, get hooked; 2) to become dependent <i>(on)</i></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсаживать.html>подса́живать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podsáživatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсадить.html>подсади́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podsadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садиться.html>сади́ться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sadítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сесть.html>сесть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

</td></tr></tbody></table><br><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>О́бщее</a> прототипическое <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:действие.html>де́йствие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́нию</a> гл. подсекать, <a href = vnd.unilang:подсечь.html>подсе́чь</a></i>.
</p>
<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="специальное"><a href = vnd.unilang:спец.html>спец</a>.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="устаревшее">устар.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чего́</a></span> вырубание (<a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>дере́вьев</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>чтобы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очистить.html>очи́стить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>место</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пашня.html>па́шни</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсечка.html>Подсе́чка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>леса</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li>срезание чего-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:снизу.html>сни́зу</a>, подрезание (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:растение.html>расте́нии</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́реве</a>) <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:древний.html>дре́вней</a> Греции <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсечка.html>подсе́чкой</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:хвойный.html>хво́йных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>дере́вьев</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:добывать.html>добыва́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:канифоль.html>канифо́ль</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:живопись.html>жи́вописи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:декоративный.html>декорати́вных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:украшение.html>украше́ниях</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:использовать.html>испо́льзовали</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ценный.html>це́нную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смола.html>смолу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мастика.html>масти́ке</a>. </span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подсказывать.html>подска́зывавший</a> (6419)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подсказывать.html>подска́зывать</a> (6419)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсказать.html>подсказа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podskazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсказывать.html>подска́зывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podskázyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсказать.html>подсказа́ть</a></b>)

***подскакивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подскакивать.html>подска́кивать</a> (15928)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подскок-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podskok-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подскок-</span> is the underlying stem of perfective verb <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подскочить.html>подскочи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podskočítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whose surface stem is affected by iotation.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подскакивать.html>подска́кивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podskákivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подскочить.html>подскочи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to jump up</li>
<li>to skyrocket (e.g. of prices)</li>
<li>to come running</li></ol>

***подскочить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подскочить.html>подскочи́ть</a> (6084)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-скочи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skočítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подскочить.html>подскочи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podskočítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подскакивать.html>подска́кивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to jump up</li>
<li>to skyrocket (e.g. of prices)</li>
<li>to come running</li></ol>

***подслушать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подслушать.html>подслу́шать</a> (12746)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слушать.html>слу́шать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slúšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подслушать.html>подслу́шать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podslúšatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подслушивать.html>подслу́шивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to eavesdrop, to overhear, to bug, to intercept</li></ol>

***подслушивание.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подслушивание.html>подслу́шивание</a> (28724)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подслушивать.html>подслу́шивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podslúšivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ание</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подслушивание.html>подслу́шивание</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podslúšivanije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подслушивание.html>подслу́шивания</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подслушивание.html>подслу́шивания</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подслушивание.html>подслу́шиваний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>eavesdropping <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">listening to private conversation</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smotrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
